---@param ... string
---@return scrollitemtemplate
---@commet usage : ScrollItemTemplate:Tem("Candy","happy");ScrollItemTemplate:Tem("Candy:happy")
function ScrollItemTemplate:Tem(...)
    local key = ""
    for i, v in ipairs { ... } do
        key = key == "" and v or key .. ":" .. v
    end

    local language = "english"--LocalizeUtil:GetLanguage()

    local data = self[language]
    local value = nil
    if data ~= nil then
        value = data[key]
    end
    if value == nil then
        value = self["english"][key]
    end
    return value
end

---@param ... string
---@return scrollitemtemplate[]
function ScrollItemTemplate:Lis(...)
    local key = ""
    for i, v in ipairs { ... } do
        key = key == "" and v or key .. ":" .. v
    end

	local language = "english"--LocalizeUtil:GetLanguage()
	local data = self[language]
	if data == nil then
		data = self["english"]
	end
    local list = {}
	local tempValue;
    for i, v in pairs(data) do
        if string.startswith(i, key) then
			tempValue = data[i]
			if tempValue == nil and language ~="english" then
				tempValue = self["english"][i]
			end
            list[i] = tempValue
        end
    end
    return list
end

---@return scrollitemtemplate[]
function ScrollItemTemplate:Dic()
    local language =  "english"--LocalizeUtil:GetLanguage()
    local data = self[language]
    if data == nil then
        data = self["english"]
    end
    return data
end

return ScrollItemTemplate
--return ConstClass("ScrollItemTemplate", ScrollItemTemplate)
